lavrentyii: When AI was merged into main from pre-release it introduced a pretty big bug. We were checking out the dump files from a server and the 2nd highest entity count was invariably the planner entity. This is what is used when you go to deploy anything. How could this be? Well, it turned out that this bug has been in the game forever, but AI uncovered it for us. AI would eat food and seeds ‚Äì seeds used the planner entity to figure out how they could be deployed. When the AI ate the seed, it just deleted the item which didn‚Äôt properly clean up after itself, letting an entity leak each time. This also happened anytime two stackable, equippable items were merged in the world (e.g.: throwing bandages on each other), but as this happened so infrequently, we could not detect the bug. This is all fixed now.  Tl;dr entity counts on large servers should drop by about ~50,000, and you‚Äôll see some memory usage reductions (after a wipe).

Major cities make the fps ditch to 15-25fps, in fields and islands, I'm looking at 45-65. Keep note though, it's very early days and optimisation has NOT been done. For example, the same Mac can run BF1 at 60fps locked on Ultra just fine and even GTA V maxed out at 50-90fps. All of this was displayed on a 2560x1440p 27" Apple Cinema Displa
